 matdaan khatm hone ke saath hi 11 jilon kii 67 siton par 721 ummidavaaron kii kismat iviem main lock ho gai he
 Know what were the characteristics of voting in this phase
 1
 After the second phase of voting in Uttar Pradesh, it has become clear that there is no wave in the state in favor of any party or against any party
 zyaadaatar siton par trikoniya muqabla ho rahaa he or voting khatm hone ke baad har party ko kaagaj kalam lekar hisaab lagaana pad rahaa he ki kis seat par uske haar-jeet kii kitni sambhaavna he
 The Samajwadi Party won the highest number of 34 seats in the last assembly elections in the 67 seats on Wednesday
 raajnneetik jaankaron ke mutabik sapa ke liye is baar aisa shandaar pradarshan doharaa paanaa or akele aadhi se zyada siten jeet le janaa naammumkin to nahin lekin mushkil bharaa jarur hoga
 2
 voting main dharmik dhruvikaran or jaateey sameekaran donon alag-alag jagahon par apni bhoomika nibhaate najar aate hai
 Religious polarization was witnessed in many seats in Bareilly, Moradabad, Rampur, Amroha and Bijnor
 chunavi panditon ke anusaar duusare charan kii zyaadaatar siton par bijepi majbootee se chunaav lard rahi he or adhiktar jagah par uskaa muqabla samaajawaadee party-congress gathbandhan se dikhaa, lekin jin siton par bispi ke damdaar ummidavaar bijepi ko haraa paane kii sthiti main dekhte hai, vahaan par muslim matadaata bispi ko bhi vot kar rahe hai
 In the seats where caste equations dominate more, candidates and local issues become important and the BSP seems to be in a strong position in all such places
 3
 In the second phase, all the seats where the elections were held were such, where only Muslim voters decide to win the elections to a large extent
 muslim matadaataaon ke bich vibhaajan kii bhi kaaphi ummid he
 This division may be due to different castes among Muslims in some places and candidates
 jaise is ilaake main badi sankhya main maujuud banjaaraa musalamaanon kii pehali pasand samaajawaadee party rahi he to kheti-kisaani karne vaale turki musalamaanon ne hameshaa bahujan samaaj party kaa saath diya he
 It remains to be seen who the voters have chosen at this stage
 4
 Among the 11 districts in the second phase of voting, Bijnor, Saharanpur, Moradabad, Amroha and Sambhal are the districts where Jat population is important in many seats, but unlike in the first phase, religious polarization can dominate in these places
 agar aisa hua to ajit singh kii party ko thodaa-bahut nuksaan ho saktaa he
 However, it is only a political speculation that the real picture will be clear on the day of counting
 5

 jin ilaakon main dharmik dhruvikaran hua he vahaan par daliton ke vot main send lagane kii ummid kii ja sakati he
 In some places the vote of Dalit castes like Pasi, Kori and Valmiki can also be in bjp's bag, this possibility cannot be ruled out
 6
 Apart from the sporadic Dalit votes and the support of the upper castes, the votes of the most backward castes are also likely to go to the bjp's account

 7
 pital ke udyog vaala muradabad or lakdi ke kaam ke liye mashhoor saharanpur do aisi jagahen hai jahaan par notebandi chunaav main ek pramukh mudda rahi

 lekin in donon jagahon par logon kii naaraazgi kaa zyada nuksaanbijepico nahin uthaanaa padegaa
